# GCC Optimization Pass Registration and Execution Chain

## Your Task

Trace how GCC's optimization passes are registered and executed during compilation. Find all C/C++ source files in `gcc-mirror/gcc` that: 1. Define the pass execution order (`gcc/passes.def` — the master list of all passes). 2. Implement the pass manager that orchestrates pass execution (`gcc/passes.cc`). 3. Define the `opt_pass` base class and pass manager interface (`gcc/pass_manager.h`). 4. Implement a concrete GIMPLE optimization pass — specifically dead code elimination (`gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc`). 5. Define the tree-SSA pass header (`gcc/tree-pass.h`) that declares pass registration macros. Report the repo, file path, and key struct/function name for each file.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

58-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced GCC's optimization pass registration and execution chain and created a comprehensive answer file. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Files Identified

1. **gcc/passes.def** - Master pass definition file using macros (NEXT_PASS, INSERT_PASSES_AFTER, etc.) to define pass execution order

2. **gcc/pass_manager.h** - Pass manager class that maintains pass lists and instantiated passes with member variables auto-generated from pass-instances.def

3. **gcc/tree-pass.h** - Pass infrastructure with:
   - `opt_pass` base class with gate() and execute() virtual methods
   - `gimple_opt_pass`, `rtl_opt_pass`, `simple_ipa_opt_pass`, `ipa_opt_pass_d` subclasses
   - `pass_data` structure for pass metadata

4. **gcc/passes.cc** - Pass execution engine with key functions:
   - `execute_one_pass()` - executes individual passes
   - `execute_pass_list()` - traverses and executes pass trees
   - Individual pass implementations

5. **gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc** - Concrete GIMPLE optimization pass example:
   - `pass_dce` and `pass_cd_dce` classes
   - `perform_tree_ssa_dce()` - the dead code elimination algorithm
   - `make_pass_dce()` factory function

## Execution Flow

The chain works hierarchically:
1. Compilation starts by calling `execute_pass_list()` with the root pass list
2. `execute_pass_list_1()` recursively traverses the pass tree (linear passes with sub-passes)
3. For each pass, `execute_one_pass()`:
   - Checks `pass->gate()` to see if it should run
   - Calls `pass->execute()` to execute the pass logic
   - Executes TODO items for cleanup
4. For DCE, the `perform_tree_ssa_dce()` algorithm marks and removes dead code

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json` with all files, symbols, execution chain, and detailed narrativ

Pass Definition and Registration (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/passes.def)\\nThe master pass definition file defines all optimization passes and their execution order using preprocessor macros:\\n- **NEXT_PASS(pass_name)** - adds a pass to the current list\\n- **INSERT_PASSES_AFTER(list_name)** - starts defining passes for a specific pass list\\n- **PUSH_INSERT_PASSES_WITHIN(superpass)** - begins definition of sub-passes within a superpass\\n- **POP_INSERT_PASSES()** - closes sub-pass definition\\n- **TERMINATE_PASS_LIST(list_name)** - ends a pass list\\n\\nExample pass lists defined:\\n- all_lowering_passes: Initial function lowering passes\\n- all_small_ipa_passes: Small inter-procedural analysis passes\\n- all_regular_ipa_passes: Regular IPA passes\\n- all_late_ipa_passes: Late-stage IPA passes\\n- all_passes: All general optimization passes\\n\\n### 2. Pass Infrastructure Header (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/tree-pass.h)\\nDefines the pass class hierarchy and metadata:\\n\\n**pass_data structure**: Contains metadata for a pass:\\n- type: GIMPLE_PASS, RTL_PASS, SIMPLE_IPA_PASS, or IPA_PASS\\n- name: Pass identifier string\\n- optinfo_flags: Optimization information group flags\\n- tv_id: Timevar identifier for profiling\\n- properties_required: Input properties (PROP_cfg, PROP_ssa, etc.)\\n- properties_provided: Output properties\\n- properties_destroyed: Properties invalidated by this pass\\n- todo_flags_start: Cleanup tasks before pass execution\\n- todo_flags_finish: Cleanup tasks after pass execution\\n\\n**opt_pass class**: Base class for all optimization passes:\\n- Methods:\\n  - gate(function*) - returns true if pass should execute\\n  - execute(function*) - main pass implementation\\n  - clone() - creates a copy of the pass instance\\n  - set_pass_param() - sets pass parameters\\n- Fields:\\n  - sub: pointer to first sub-pass (for hierarchical passes)\\n  - next: pointer to next pass at same level\\n  - static_pass_number: unique pass identifier\\n\\n**Pass type classes**:\\n- gimple_opt_pass: For GIMPLE-level optimization passes\\n- rtl_opt_pass: For register transfer language passes\\n- simple_ipa_opt_pass: For simple inter-procedural passes\\n- ipa_opt_pass_d: For full IPA passes with summary generation/transformation\\n\\nPass registration macros (e.g., make_pass_dce, make_pass_asan) are declared as factory functions.\\n\\n### 4. This allows:\\n- Multiple instances of the same pass (e.g., pass_copy_prop_1, pass_copy_prop_2, ...)\\n- Automatic tracking of all pass instances\\n- Direct member access to pass instances from pass_manager\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Visitor Pattern**: Pass classes implement gate() and execute() virtual methods\\n2. **Tree Structure**: Pass hierarchies enable superpass organization (sub-passes nested within parent)\\n3. **Factory Pattern**: make_pass_* functions create pass instances\\n4. **Metadata Separation**: pass_data structure separates static metadata from instance data\\n5. **TODO System**: Passes return TODO flags indicating required post-pass cleanup\\n6. **Property Tracking**: Passes declare properties_required/provided to ensure correct pass ordering\\n\"}",

Returns TODO flags for subsequent cleanup (TODO_update_ssa, TODO_cleanup_cfg)\\n\\n**Factory function** (lines 2100-2104): make_pass_dce() creates and returns a new pass_dce instance\\n\\n## Execution Flow Chain\\n\\nThe complete execution chain from compilation driver through pass execution:\\n\\n1. **Compilation Start** (in cgraphunit.cc):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list(cfun, g->get_passes()->all_passes)\\n\\n2. **Pass List Traversal** (execute_pass_list):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list_1(pass) to recursively traverse pass tree\\n\\n3. **Pass Tree Recursion** (execute_pass_list_1):\\n   - For each pass:\\n     - Calls execute_one_pass(pass)\\n     - If succeeded and pass->sub exists, recursively calls execute_pass_list_1(pass->sub)\\n     - Moves to next sibling (pass->next)\\n\\n4. **Individual Pass Execution** (execute_one_pass):\\n   - Checks pass->gate(cfun) - determines if pass should run\\n   - Calls pass->execute(cfun) - executes pass logic\\n   - For DCE pass: execute() calls execute_dce(func, aggressive)\\n\\n5. **DCE Algorithm** (perform_tree_ssa_dce):\\n   - Marks statements as necessary based on control/data dependencies\\n   - Propagates necessity through use-def chains\\n   - Eliminates unmarked dead statements\\n   - Returns TODO flags for SSA/CFG updates\\n\\n6. **Pass Cleanup**:\\n   - Executes TODO items (SSA rebuilding, CFG cleanup)\\n   - Publishes pass completion event\\n   - Returns to pass loop for next pass\\n\\n## Pass Instance Generation\\n\\nThe system uses AWK script (gen-pass-instances.awk) to process passes.def and generate pass-instances.def, which defines member variables in pass_manager for each pass instance. This allows:\\n- Multiple instances of the same pass (e.g., pass_copy_prop_1, pass_copy_prop_2, ...)\\n- Automatic tracking of all pass instances\\n- Direct member access to pass instances from pass_manager\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Visitor Pattern**: Pass classes implement gate() and execute() virtual methods\\n2. **Tree Structure**: Pass hierarchies enable superpass organization (sub-passes nested within parent)\\n3. **Factory Pattern**: make_pass_* functions create pass instances\\n4. **Metadata Separation**: pass_data structure separates static metadata from instance data\\n5. **TODO System**: Passes return TODO flags indicating required post-pass cleanup\\n6. **Property Tracking**: Passes declare properties_required/provided to ensure correct pass ordering\\n\"}",
